UI Preview Quality Rules

‡∏Å‡∏é Visual Design ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á HTML Preview ‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á ‚Äî ‡∏™‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Refactoring UI, Practical UI, Laws of UX, Don't Make Me Think, Design of Everyday Things, Designing Interfaces + 60 ‡πÄ‡∏•‡πà‡∏° (ytx-readings/design-ui-ux + justinhartman/ui-ux-design-library)

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á HTML Preview, ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à QA, Review Design, ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Handoff Spec

1. Visual Hierarchy (‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Refactoring UI + NNGroup)

‡∏Å‡∏é Hierarchy

  • Size ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ font weight + color + spacing ‡∏£‡πà‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô
  • De-emphasize ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ emphasize ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å ‚Äî ‡∏•‡∏î contrast/weight ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á secondary content
  • Labels ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏ó‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢ ‚Äî ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤ visual design ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏û‡∏≠ ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ label
  • 3 ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö hierarchy ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏û‡∏≠ ‚Äî Primary, Secondary, Tertiary (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô 3 size levels)
  • CTA ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á pop ‚Äî Von Restorff Effect: ‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÅ‡∏ï‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏ï

Reading Patterns

  • F-Pattern: ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö content-heavy (list, feed) ‚Äî ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏î‡πÅ‡∏£‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏ï‡πá‡∏° ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß scan ‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏á‡∏°‡∏≤
  • Z-Pattern: ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö landing page ‚Äî ‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏ô ‚Üí ‡∏Ç‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏ö‡∏ô ‚Üí ‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á ‚Üí ‡∏Ç‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á (CTA ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ç‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á)

2. Color Rules (‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Refactoring UI + Color Theory books)

‡∏û‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô

  • 60-30-10: 60% neutral (bg), 30% secondary, 10% accent (CTA)
  • ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î 3 ‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å + shades (9-10 shades ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠ hue)
  • ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ HSL ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà hex ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á shade ‚Äî ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö saturation + lightness ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ intuitive
  • Near-black/near-white ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô pure #000/#FFF ‚Äî ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô #1B1D22 ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô #000000
  • Neutral ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á gray ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡πâ ‚Äî ‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏° warm/cool hue ‡πÄ‡∏•‡πá‡∏Å‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢ (saturation < 5% ‡πÉ‡∏ô HSB)
  • ‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á hue ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ distinct brightness ‚Äî ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô visual competition
  • Saturate neutrals ‡∏ó‡∏¥‡∏®‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß ‚Äî warm ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ cool ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ú‡∏™‡∏°

Semantic Colors (‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏•)

‡∏™‡∏µ ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö
Red Error, destructive, urgent Success, neutral info
Green Success, positive, confirm Error, warning
Yellow/Amber Warning, caution Error, success
Blue Info, primary action, links Error, warning

Dark Mode Rules

  • ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà invert ‡∏™‡∏µ ‚Äî ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á reduce contrast, ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ muted colors
  • Container brightness ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô 12% (HSB) ‡πÉ‡∏ô dark mode, 7% ‡πÉ‡∏ô light mode
  • Lighter = ‡πÉ‡∏Å‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ ‚Äî surface ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà "‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏¢" ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏™‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ background
  • ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ shadow ‡πÉ‡∏ô dark mode ‚Äî ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏‡∏ú‡∏•‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô
  • Font ‡πÄ‡∏•‡πá‡∏Å ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô ‡πÉ‡∏ô dark mode ‚Äî ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° weight ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ size

3. Typography Rules (‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Refactoring UI + Typography books)

Scale

  • Proportional type scale ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ ratio ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô 1.25) ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î
  • Body text >= 16px ‚Äî ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏•‡πá‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏ô mobile
  • Max 2 typefaces ‚Äî heading + body (‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏Å‡πá‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤ weight ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô)
  • 2-3 weights ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏û‡∏≠ ‚Äî Regular, Semibold/Bold, Heavy (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å weight)

Readability

  • Line length 60-80 characters (optimal: 66) ‚Äî ‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢
  • Line-height ‡∏™‡∏±‡∏°‡∏û‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ò‡πå‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö size ‚Äî text ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà = line-height ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏á, text ‡πÄ‡∏•‡πá‡∏Å = line-height ‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô
  • Letter-spacing ‡∏™‡∏±‡∏°‡∏û‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ò‡πå‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö size ‚Äî heading ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á negative tracking
  • Left-aligned ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠ (Thai + English) ‚Äî ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏° justify (‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å)
  • All caps ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞ labels/buttons ‡∏™‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÜ ‚Äî ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö paragraph

Links & Text

  • ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å link ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ underline ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ weight ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ
  • ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏•‡∏î contrast ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ de-emphasize text ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ font size/weight ‡πÄ‡∏•‡πá‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô (contrast ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≥ = ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å)

4. Spacing Rules (‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Refactoring UI + Grid Systems)

System

  • ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ spacing system ‚Äî ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà mathematically related (4px grid: 4, 8, 12, 16, 20, 24, 32, 40, 48)
  • ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å space ‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏õ ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏î ‚Äî ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏ô‡πà‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°
  • ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏ï‡πá‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏û‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà ‚Äî white space ‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠ design element

Relationships

  • Outer padding >= Inner padding ‚Äî padding ‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏Å container ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á >= padding ‡πÉ‡∏ô container
  • ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏î spacing ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á high-contrast edges ‚Äî ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà center-to-center
  • ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏° ambiguous spacing ‚Äî ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ element ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô (Gestalt: Proximity)
  • Spacing ratio: related items = 1x, semi-related = 2x, sections = 3-4x, major sections = 5-6x

Layout

  • 12-column grid ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö horizontal layouts ‚Äî divisible by 2, 3, 4, 6
  • Grids are overrated ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ flexible spacing logic ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ strict grid ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏ì‡∏µ
  • Content ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ï‡πá‡∏° width ‚Äî max-width ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢ readability

5. Borders & Separation (‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Refactoring UI)

  • ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ border ‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏á ‚Äî ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ box-shadow, background contrast, ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ spacing
  • Container border ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á contrast ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á fill AND background ‚Äî ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß
  • ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏°‡∏µ adjacent hard divides ‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô ‚Äî background transition + container edge + dividing line ‡πÉ‡∏ô 1 ‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î = ‡∏£‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏õ

6. Shadows & Depth (‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Refactoring UI + Practical UI)

  • ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏á‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏¥‡∏®‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß ‚Äî consistent ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤
  • Shadow blur = 2x distance value ‚Äî ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô offset-y: 4px ‚Üí blur: 8px
  • ‡∏•‡∏î opacity ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ element ‡πÉ‡∏Å‡∏•‡πâ viewer ‚Äî elevated element ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏°‡∏µ shadow ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤
  • ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ shadow approach ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á project ‚Äî ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ú‡∏™‡∏° soft/hard/no-shadow
  • ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ shadow ‡πÉ‡∏ô dark mode ‚Äî ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏°‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô
  • Lighter = ‡πÉ‡∏Å‡∏•‡πâ ‚Äî ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á light mode ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ dark mode

7. Button Design (‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Refactoring UI + Practical UI)

  • Horizontal padding = 2x Vertical padding ‚Äî ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô padding: 12px 24px
  • Button hierarchy ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô ‚Äî Primary (solid, bold color) > Secondary (outlined/muted) > Tertiary (text only)
  • High contrast ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö important elements ‚Äî minimal contrast ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö structural elements
  • Gray button ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏î‡∏π‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô disabled ‚Äî ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏™‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô secondary button

8. Corner Radius (‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Practical UI)

  • Nested radius = outer radius - gap ‚Äî ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤ outer = 16px, gap = 8px ‚Üí inner = 8px
  • Consistent radius ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á app ‚Äî ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ú‡∏™‡∏° sharp + rounded ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏‡∏ú‡∏•

9. Icons (‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å NNGroup + Refactoring UI)

  • ‡∏•‡∏î contrast ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á icon ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏π‡πà‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö text ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ opacity ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ text
  • Icon ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ text label ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠ ‚Äî "word is worth a thousand pictures"
  • ‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà 3 icon ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà universal: home, print, magnifying glass ‚Äî ‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô‡πÜ ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ label
  • ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏î icon ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏ô 5 ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ ‚Äî concept ‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ã‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ icon ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ

10. Component Patterns (‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Designing Interfaces + Practical UI)

Cards

  • ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö browsing heterogeneous content (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö search/comparison)
  • Variable height, consistent width ‚Äî ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà force ‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î
  • Summary + link pattern: condensed teaser ‚Üí fuller details

Forms

  • Label ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏î ‚Äî ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ placeholder ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô label
  • Floating labels ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ issues ‚Äî visible label ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠
  • Placeholder = hint format ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà label (strain short-term memory, ‡∏™‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö default value)
  • Error ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÉ‡∏Å‡∏•‡πâ input ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏™‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏î‡∏á + icon + text (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏™‡∏µ)
  • ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏•‡∏ö input ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà user ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î error ‚Äî preserve user input ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠

Toggles

  • Immediate effect ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏î Save ‚Äî ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á Save ‚Üí ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ radio/checkbox ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô
  • Label ‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢ ON state ‚Äî ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°

Modals

  • ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô user engage ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö content
  • ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡∏±‡∏î‡∏à‡∏±‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ß‡∏∞ critical task ‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á
  • ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô modal ‚Äî popup ‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ö popup = nightmare
  • Focus trap ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö modal dialog ‚Äî keyboard ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ô modal

Empty States

  • ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏õ‡∏•‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á ‚Äî ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ: status message + learning cue + actionable pathway
  • ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏™ ‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ô user ‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ feature ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£

‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏¢‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤ Pattern Notes
< 1 ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏™‡∏∂‡∏Å instant

11. Accessibility Quick Rules

  • Text contrast >= 4.5:1 (WCAG AA) ‚Äî ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏π‡πà‡∏™‡∏µ
  • Touch target >= 44px + spacing >= 2mm (8px)
  • ‡∏™‡∏µ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ö‡πà‡∏á‡∏ä‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß ‚Äî ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ icon/shape/text ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢
  • Focus indicator ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î (contrast >= 3:1)
  • ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö prefers-reduced-motion ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å animation

12. Animation Rules

  • ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å animation ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ purpose ‚Äî guide attention, show connection, provide feedback
  • User-triggered < 0.1s ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô ‚Äî Doherty Threshold
  • Animation ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏•‡πà‡∏ô‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô roadblock ‚Äî ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏° force animation ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà user ‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢
  • Background = ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤, Foreground = ‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ ‚Äî direct interaction ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏ß
  • No animation > bad animation ‚Äî ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏‡∏ú‡∏• ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏µ
  • Reduced-motion alternative ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠

13. UX Writing Quick Rules (‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Don't Make Me Think + Strategic Writing)

  • User scan ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô ‚Äî ‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö scanning (F/Z pattern)
  • 2 ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á heading/link ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î ‚Äî front-load keyword
  • Plain language ‚Äî ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏µ‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á jargon ‡πÅ‡∏°‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö expert audience
  • Error = ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤ + ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏¥
  • Button = action verb ‚Äî "‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å" ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà "‡∏ï‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏á"
  • Link = promise ‚Äî text ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏õ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô (‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏° "Click here", "Learn More")
  • ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏Ç‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ digits ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏≥ ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ digital

14. Don't Make Me Think ‚Äî Core Principles

  1. Self-evident > Self-explanatory > Need explanation ‚Äî ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏î ‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏û‡∏≠
  2. ‡∏•‡∏î noise ‚Äî ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å element ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏Ç‡πà‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö element ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô
  3. Create clear visual hierarchy ‚Äî ‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á look important
  4. Convention ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ innovation ‚Äî ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤ standard pattern ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏î‡∏¥‡∏©‡∏ê‡πå‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà (Jakob's Law)
  5. Omit needless words ‚Äî ‡∏•‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏° 50% ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏Å 50%

15. Laws of UX ‚Äî Quick Reference

Law ‡∏Å‡∏é 1 ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏î ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ô Preview
Aesthetic-Usability ‡∏™‡∏ß‡∏¢ = ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ (‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ) Polish visual details
Hick's Law ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å = ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏î‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏à‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏≤ ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î CTA/options ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠ section
Fitts's Law ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà + ‡πÉ‡∏Å‡∏•‡πâ = ‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ CTA ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà‡∏û‡∏≠ + ‡πÉ‡∏Å‡∏•‡πâ cursor
Miller's Law ‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ 7¬±2 items chunk ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° 5-9
Jakob's Law ‡∏ä‡∏≠‡∏ö pattern ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏¢ follow platform conventions
Doherty Threshold < 400ms = flow state skeleton screens, instant feedback
Von Restorff ‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏≥ CTA ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á
Serial Position ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÅ‡∏£‡∏Å + ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏ó‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢ ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô + ‡∏ó‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢ list
Peak-End Rule peak + ending = ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≥ optimize ‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î + ‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏à‡∏ö
Proximity ‡πÉ‡∏Å‡∏•‡πâ = ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á spacing ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á group ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å
Similarity ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô = ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏†‡∏ó‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô consistent styling = same meaning
Occam's Razor ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î ‡∏ä‡∏ô‡∏∞ ‡∏•‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà serve user goal
Tesler's Law complexity ‡∏•‡∏î‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ ‡∏ã‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô complexity ‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà user

MASTER CHECKLIST ‚Äî ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏™‡πà‡∏á Preview

Visual Quality

  • Typography ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ defined scale (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏™‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°)
  • Body text >= 16px; line length 60-80 chars
  • Line-height ‡∏™‡∏±‡∏°‡∏û‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ò‡πå‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö text size
  • Max 2 typefaces, 2-3 weights
  • Spacing ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ 4px grid system
  • Outer padding >= inner padding
  • ‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å palette ‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô; 60-30-10 ratio
  • Near-black/near-white (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà pure #000/#FFF)
  • Neutral greys ‡∏°‡∏µ subtle hue shift
  • Shadows consistent ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å single light source
  • Shadow blur = 2x distance
  • Nested corner radius = outer - gap
  • ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ adjacent hard divides ‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô

Hierarchy & Composition

  • Visual hierarchy ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô 3 ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö
  • CTA ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏î‡πà‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏ö‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤
  • Gestalt grouping ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á (proximity, similarity, common region)
  • F/Z reading pattern ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å guide ‡πÑ‡∏õ CTA

Interaction Quality

  • Interactive elements ‡∏°‡∏µ affordance ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô
  • Button hierarchy: Primary > Secondary > Tertiary
  • Button padding: horizontal = 2x vertical
  • Touch targets >= 44px + spacing >= 8px
  • ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å state ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ö: default, hover, pressed, focused, disabled, error, loading
  • Toggle = immediate effect (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á Save)
  • Form labels ‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏î (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ focus)
  • Error = adjacent + red + icon + problem + solution

Accessibility

  • Text contrast >= 4.5:1 (AA)
  • ‡∏™‡∏µ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ö‡πà‡∏á‡∏ä‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß
  • Icon ‡∏°‡∏µ text label
  • Focus indicators ‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î
  • Reduced-motion alternatives

Content & UX Writing

  • Heading: keyword-first, scannable
  • Button: action verbs (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà "‡∏ï‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏á/OK")
  • Error: non-judgmental, constructive
  • Empty state: status + learning + action
  • Link text: specific (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà "Click here")
  • Numbers: digits ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏≥

Performance Perception

  • Skeleton screens ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö 2-10s loads
  • No skeleton ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö < 1s
  • Progress bar ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö > 10s
  • Animation ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ô < 0.1s
  • ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ gratuitous/repeated animation

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î Brand Voice ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö ‚Äî ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å dimension ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á "‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà" ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ "‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà":

Pattern 4: Empty States

  • ‡∏™‡∏π‡∏ï‡∏£: "‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ [‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå] ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ [‡∏ó‡∏≥ action]"

# Heuristic ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏° ‡∏Ñ‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏ô (1-5)

Internet Language Conventions (From "Because Internet")

Tone Indicators ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏Ñ‡∏î‡∏¥‡∏à‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏•

  • Period (.): ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô "." ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏™‡∏∂‡∏Å "‡πÇ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏ò" ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ "‡πÄ‡∏¢‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ä‡∏≤" ‚Üí ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞ UI formal, ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô chat/toast

Formal vs Informal Spectrum

FORMAL ‚Üê‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚Üí INFORMAL
Legal    Banking    E-com    Social    Gaming    Chat

‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö voice ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° product type:

  • Formal (Banking, Legal): ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ contractions, ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ emoji, ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ full sentences
  • Neutral (E-com, Productivity): Contractions OK, no emoji in errors, sentence fragments OK
  • Informal (Social, Gaming): Emoji OK, slang OK in moderation, fragments encouraged

# Figma UI Design Specification Skill

‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£ UI Design Specification ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏ô ‡∏≠‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° preview ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ

## Pipeline Position

```
Jira BA ‚Üí IA + User Flow ‚Üí [UI Design] ‚Üí QA Gate ‚Üí ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏ö
                              ‚ñ≤ ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ
```

## Overall Flow

```
1. Requirements ‚Üí 2. Read Design Principles ‚Üí 3. Preview (HTML) ‚Üí 4. Iterate (Browser) ‚Üí 5. QA Gate ‚Üí 6. Import to Figma (HTML to Figma MCP)
```

‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á 6 ‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠ flow ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á skill:

1. **Requirements**: ‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ (‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Jira card ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô jira-req-analysis ‚Üí figma-user-flow pipeline)
2. **Design Principles**: ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô references ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£
3. **Preview**: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Static HTML file (.html) ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏î‡∏π‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô browser ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô import ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤ Figma
4. **Iterate**: User ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î HTML ‡πÉ‡∏ô browser + ‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏Å Claude ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç ‚Üí refresh ‡∏î‡∏π‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ
5. **QA Gate**: ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á HTML ‡πÑ‡∏õ **html-qa-gate** skill ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û (Color, Accessibility, Navigation, Sizing, Spacing) ‚Äî auto-fix + ‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à max 3 ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ö
6. **Import to Figma**: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ html-to-design MCP ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á HTML ‡πÑ‡∏õ Figma ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á (`import_html` / `import_url`)

---

## Step 1: ‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏° Requirements

Requirements ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å:
- **IA + User Flow pipeline** ‚Üí ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤ user ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô `jira-req-analysis` ‚Üí `figma-user-flow` pipeline ‡∏°‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏µ structured data ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ö: Screen Map, Navigation Matrix, User Flows (happy + error paths), Feature Inventory, User Stories, State Matrix ‚Äî ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÑ‡∏õ Step 2 ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¢
- **Jira card analysis** ‚Üí ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤ user ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô `jira-req-analysis` skill ‡∏°‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏µ structured data (User Stories, Screen List, State Matrix, Components, User Flow) ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ ‚Äî ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÑ‡∏õ Step 2 ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¢
- **User ‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á** ‚Üí ‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á
- **Figma reference design** ‚Üí ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ get_screenshot/get_design_context ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô

‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ structured requirements ‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ:

- **Platform**: Mobile (iOS/Android), Web, Desktop, ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Cross-platform?
- **Screen/Component**: ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ component ‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£?
- **User Goal**: ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ?
- **Detail Level**: ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Wireframe (Lo-fi) ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Hi-fi UI spec?
- **Design System**: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Material Design, HIG, ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ custom design system?
- **Constraints**: ‡∏°‡∏µ brand guidelines, ‡∏™‡∏µ, font ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- **Reference Design**: ‡∏°‡∏µ Figma URL ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏î‡∏π‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô reference ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°? (‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ get_screenshot/get_design_context ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ)

---

## Step 2: ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô Design Principles

‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô reference files ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° platform:

```
references/ux-principles.md        ‚Üí ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠ (Nielsen's + Laws of UX + Gestalt)
references/material-design.md      ‚Üí ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Android / Web (Material Design 3)
references/hig.md                  ‚Üí ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö iOS / macOS (Apple HIG)
references/design-tokens.md        ‚Üí ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Custom Design System tokens
```

‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô `references/ux-principles.md` **‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á**
‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô `references/ui-preview-quality-rules.md` **‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á** ‚Äî ‡∏Å‡∏é Visual Design ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Refactoring UI, Practical UI, Laws of UX, Don't Make Me Think

‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö platform-specific:
- Android / Material ‚Üí ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° `references/material-design.md`
- iOS / Apple ‚Üí ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° `references/hig.md`
- Cross-platform ‚Üí ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå

‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏°‡∏µ reference design URL:
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `get_screenshot(fileKey, nodeId)` ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏π visual
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `get_design_context(fileKey, nodeId)` ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô design details
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `get_metadata(fileKey, nodeId)` ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏π structure

---

## Step 3: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Interactive Preview (Static HTML)

‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå `.html` self-contained ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ô browser ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô import ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤ Figma

### Preview ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ:

1. **iPhone/Android frame** ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô 393x852 ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö iPhone 15 Pro) ‚Äî CSS-only
2. **Status bar** ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á (‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤, battery, signal) ‚Äî HTML+CSS
3. **‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å component** ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° spec ‚Äî ‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Design Tokens (CSS Variables)
4. **Light/Dark mode toggle** ‡∏™‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö theme ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ (vanilla JS)
5. **State switcher** ‚Äî ‡∏õ‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô state: empty, filled, error, loading, success (vanilla JS)
6. **Interactive elements** ‚Äî ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å input, ‡∏Å‡∏î‡∏õ‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° ‡∏î‡∏π state ‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á (vanilla JS)
7. **Spec info panel** ‚Äî ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç (frame size, font, spacing, colors)

### HTML Template:

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="th">
<head>
  <meta charset="UTF-8">
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
  <title>[Screen Name] Preview</title>
  <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=LINE+Seed+Sans+TH:wght@400;700;800&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
  <style>
    :root {
      /* Design Tokens ‚Äî ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å semantic system (references/design-tokens.md) */
      --primary-fg-high: #EC599D;
      --primary-fg-low: #FDEFF5;
      --primary-bg-mid: #EC599D;
      --primary-bg-low: #FBD5E5;
      --primary-bg-lowest: #FDEFF5;
      --secondary-fg-high: #7279FB;
      --secondary-bg-mid: #7279FB;
      --secondary-bg-lowest: #EEEFFE;
      --gray-fg-high: #1B1D22;
      --gray-fg-mid-on-white: #6A6E83;
      --gray-fg-mid-on-gray: #3F414E;
      --gray-fg-low: #9A9DAD;
      --gray-fg-white: #FFFFFF;
      --gray-bg-white: #FFFFFF;
      --gray-bg-lightgray: #F8F8F9;
      --gray-bg-midgray: #EBECEF;
      --gray-bg-darkgray: #CFD1D9;
      --gray-bg-black: #1B1D22;
      --gray-border-midgray: #EBECEF;
      --gray-border-darkgray: #CFD1D9;
      --error-fg-high: #EA244F;
      --error-bg-lowest: #FDECF0;
      --warning-fg-high: #F8C135;
      --warning-bg-lowest: #FEF8E8;
      --success-fg-high: #559652;
      --success-bg-lowest: #EEF6EE;
      --info-fg-high: #0386B3;
      --info-bg-lowest: #E6F4F9;

      /* Typography ‚Äî LINE Seed Sans TH (‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö Figma Text Styles) */
      --font-family: 'LINE Seed Sans TH', sans-serif;
      --heading-1: 800 48px/58px var(--font-family);   /* Heading.1 */
      --heading-2: 700 40px/52px var(--font-family);   /* Heading.2 */
      --heading-3: 700 32px/40px var(--font-family);   /* Heading.3 */
      --heading-4: 700 28px/36px var(--font-family);   /* Heading.4 */
      --heading-5: 700 24px/32px var(--font-family);   /* Heading.5 */
      --label-1: 700 20px/28px var(--font-family);     /* Label.1 */
      --label-2: 700 18px/26px var(--font-family);     /* Label.2 */
      --label-3: 700 16px/24px var(--font-family);     /* Label.3 */
      --label-4: 700 14px/22px var(--font-family);     /* Label.4 */
      --label-5: 700 12px/20px var(--font-family);     /* Label.5 */
      --caption-1: 400 20px/36px var(--font-family);   /* Caption.1 */
      --caption-2: 400 18px/26px var(--font-family);   /* Caption.2 */
      --caption-3: 400 16px/24px var(--font-family);   /* Caption.3 */
      --caption-4: 400 14px/22px var(--font-family);   /* Caption.4 */
      --caption-5: 400 12px/20px var(--font-family);   /* Caption.5 */

      /* Spacing */
      --space-xs: 4px;
      --space-sm: 8px;
      --space-md: 12px;
      --space-lg: 16px;
      --space-xl: 20px;
      --space-2xl: 24px;
      --space-3xl: 32px;

      /* Shape */
      --radius-sm: 8px;
      --radius-md: 12px;
      --radius-lg: 16px;
      --radius-full: 9999px;
    }

    * { margin: 0; padding: 0; box-sizing: border-box; }
    body { font-family: var(--font-family); background: #E5E5E5; display: flex; justify-content: center; padding: 20px; }

    /* ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ flexbox layout (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ absolute positioning) */
    /* ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ semantic HTML: header, main, nav, section, footer */
    /* Class names ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢ (‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Figma layer names) */
  </style>
</head>
<body>
  <!-- Phone Frame -->
  <div class="phone-frame" style="width:393px; min-height:852px; background:var(--gray-bg-white); border-radius:40px; overflow:hidden; box-shadow:0 8px 32px rgba(0,0,0,0.12); display:flex; flex-direction:column;">
    <!-- Status Bar -->
    <div class="status-bar" style="display:flex; justify-content:space-between; align-items:center; padding:12px 24px; font:var(--caption-4); color:var(--gray-fg-high);">
      <span>9:41</span>
      <span><!-- signal + wifi + battery icons --></span>
    </div>

    <!-- Main Content -->
    <main style="flex:1; display:flex; flex-direction:column; padding:0 var(--space-lg);">
      <!-- Content here -->
    </main>
  </div>

  <!-- Control Panel (outside phone frame) -->
  <div class="control-panel" style="margin-left:24px; padding:16px; background:white; border-radius:12px; height:fit-content;">
    <button onclick="toggleTheme()">Light/Dark</button>
    <button onclick="setState('default')">Default</button>
    <button onclick="setState('filled')">Filled</button>
    <button onclick="setState('error')">Error</button>
    <button onclick="setState('loading')">Loading</button>
    <button onclick="setState('success')">Success</button>
    <button onclick="setState('empty')">Empty</button>
  </div>

  <script>
    // Vanilla JS ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö toggle, state switch, interactions
    let currentTheme = 'light';
    let currentState = 'default';

    function toggleTheme() {
      currentTheme = currentTheme === 'light' ? 'dark' : 'light';
      document.body.setAttribute('data-theme', currentTheme);
      // Update CSS variables for dark mode
    }

    function setState(state) {
      currentState = state;
      document.querySelectorAll('[data-state]').forEach(el => {
        el.style.display = el.dataset.state === state ? '' : 'none';
      });
    }
  </script>
</body>
</html>
```

### Preview Quality Rules (‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö ‚Äî ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å references/ui-preview-quality-rules.md):

**Visual Hierarchy:**
- De-emphasize ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á (‡∏•‡∏î weight/color) ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ emphasize ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å
- 3 ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö hierarchy ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏û‡∏≠ ‚Äî Primary, Secondary, Tertiary
- CTA ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á pop ‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á (Von Restorff Effect)

**Color:**
- Near-black/near-white ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô pure #000/#FFF (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô #1B1D22 ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô #000)
- 60-30-10 ratio: neutral 60%, secondary 30%, accent 10%
- Neutral greys ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏°‡∏µ subtle warm/cool hue shift

**Typography:**
- Line-height ‡∏™‡∏±‡∏°‡∏û‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ò‡πå‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö size ‚Äî text ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà = line-height ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏á
- ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏•‡∏î contrast ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ de-emphasize ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ size/weight ‡πÄ‡∏•‡πá‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô
- Line length 60-80 chars (‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ max-width ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢)

**Spacing:**
- ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å space ‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏õ ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏î
- Outer padding >= Inner padding ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠
- ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏°‡∏µ ambiguous spacing ‚Äî ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ element ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô

**Shadows:**
- Shadow blur = 2x distance (offset-y: 4px ‚Üí blur: 8px)
- ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏á‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏¥‡∏®‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤
- ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ shadow ‡πÉ‡∏ô dark mode

**Borders:**
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ border ‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏á ‚Äî ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ shadow, background contrast, spacing
- ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏° adjacent hard divides ‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô

**Buttons:**
- Horizontal padding = 2x Vertical padding (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô padding: 12px 24px)
- Primary (solid) > Secondary (outlined) > Tertiary (text only)

**Corner Radius:**
- Nested radius = outer radius - gap (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô outer 16px, gap 8px ‚Üí inner 8px)

**Components:**
- Empty state ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏õ‡∏•‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á ‚Äî ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ status + learning cue + action
- Form labels ‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏î ‚Äî ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ placeholder ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô label
- Error = adjacent to input + icon + problem + solution
- Toggle = immediate effect (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏î Save)

### Guidelines ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö HTML Preview:

- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ **CSS Variables** ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° Design Tokens (`references/design-tokens.md`) ‚Äî ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏° hardcode ‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ **flexbox/grid** layout (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ absolute position) ‚Üí ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Auto Layout ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma
- ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á **class names** ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢ ‚Üí ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Figma layer names
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ **semantic HTML**: `<header>`, `<main>`, `<nav>`, `<section>`, `<footer>`
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ **Google Fonts** (LINE Seed Sans TH) ‚Äî load ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô `<link>`
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ **inline SVG** ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ placeholder ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö icons/images
- **‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ** external CSS frameworks (Bootstrap, Tailwind) ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ CSS ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡πÜ
- **‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ** React, Vue, ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ JS framework ‡πÉ‡∏î‡πÜ ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ vanilla JS ‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô
- Animation ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ **CSS keyframes** ‡πÉ‡∏ô `<style>` tag
- Keep DOM structure clean ‚Üí clean Figma layer hierarchy

### HTML Best Practices ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö HTML to Figma:

| HTML/CSS | Figma Result |
|----------|-------------|
| `display: flex` | Auto Layout |
| `flex-direction: column` | Vertical Auto Layout |
| `gap: 16px` | Item Spacing = 16 |
| `padding: 16px` | Padding = 16 |
| `border-radius: 12px` | Corner Radius = 12 |
| `width: 100%` (‡πÉ‡∏ô flex child) | Layout Sizing = Fill |
| Class name (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô `login-button`) | Layer name = "login-button" |
| Nested `<div>` | Nested frames |

### ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå: `[screen-name]-preview.html`

1. **User ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î `.html` ‡πÉ‡∏ô browser** ‚Äî double-click ‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Live Preview ‡πÉ‡∏ô VSCode

4. **‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏û‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏à** ‚Äî ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö layout, ‡∏™‡∏µ, ‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î, spacing, state ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÜ

## Step 5: QA Gate ‚Äî ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏ö

‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ user ‡∏û‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏à‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö HTML preview ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß **‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô QA Gate ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô import ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤ Figma**:

5. ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á 3 ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ö ‚Üí ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á report ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ user ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏î‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏à

> "‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô import ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤ Figma ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û HTML ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö ‚Äî ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πá‡∏Ñ Color, Accessibility, Sizing, Spacing"

## Step 6: Import ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤ Figma (HTML to Figma MCP)

‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏û‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏à‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö HTML preview ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ **html-to-design MCP** ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á HTML ‡πÑ‡∏õ Figma ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á

### 5.1 ‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏°‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß

1. ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ user ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î **html.to.design** plugin ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma ‚Üí tab **MCP** ‚Üí toggle **"Enable MCP endpoint"** ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà (STATUS: connected)
2. ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ HTML file ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° import:
   - ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ flexbox/grid (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ absolute position)
   - Class names ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢
   - ‡∏™‡∏µ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ CSS Variables
   - DOM structure clean

### 5.2 Import ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô MCP

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `import_html` ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á HTML ‡πÑ‡∏õ Figma ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á:

```
import_html({
  html: "<div class='login-screen'>...</div>",
  css: ".login-screen { display: flex; ... }",
  name: "Login Screen"
})
```

‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤ HTML ‡∏ã‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô/‡∏°‡∏µ external assets ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ serve file ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `import_url`:

```
import_url({
  url: "http://localhost:3000/login-preview.html",
  name: "Login Screen"
})
```

Plugin ‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á HTML ‚Üí Figma layers:
- `display: flex` ‚Üí Auto Layout
- `gap` ‚Üí Item Spacing
- `padding` ‚Üí Padding
- `border-radius` ‚Üí Corner Radius
- Class names ‚Üí Layer names
- Colors ‚Üí Fill colors
- Text ‚Üí Text nodes with font size/weight

### 5.3 Fine-tune ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma

‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á import:
1. ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à Auto Layout structure ‚Äî ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö sizing mode (FILL/HUG/FIXED)
2. ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à font ‚Äî ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô LINE Seed Sans TH ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma
3. ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à colors ‚Äî ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö HTML preview
4. ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö layer names ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£
5. ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° components, variants, styles ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£

## Design Spec Templates

‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£ spec ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å preview ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á `.md` ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° template:

### Wireframe (Lo-fi) Template

```markdown
# [Screen Name] ‚Äî Wireframe Specification

## 1. Overview
## 2. Layout Structure (with ASCII wireframe)
## 3. Component List (table)
## 4. Navigation Flow
## 5. UX Principles Applied (table with principle + rationale)
## 6. Notes for Figma Implementation
```

### Hi-fi Template

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Wireframe template + ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°:

```markdown
## 7. Visual Design (Colors, Typography, Spacing, Elevation)
## 8. Design Tokens (‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ custom design system)
## 9. Component Specifications (‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å state: default, hover, pressed, focused, disabled, error)
## 10. Accessibility (contrast, touch targets, VoiceOver/TalkBack labels)
## 11. Responsive Behavior
## 12. Motion & Haptic (iOS)
```

## WCAG Color Contrast Checker (‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö)

‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏µ **‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö WCAG Color Contrast** ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô:

### ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏ì‡∏ë‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô (WCAG 2.1)

| ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏†‡∏ó | AA (‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≥) | AAA (‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥) |
|--------|-------------|-------------|
| Normal text (< 18pt) | 4.5:1 | 7:1 |
| Large text (>= 18pt bold / >= 24pt regular) | 3:1 | 4.5:1 |
| UI components & icons | 3:1 | ‚Äî |

### ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì Contrast Ratio

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏™‡∏π‡∏ï‡∏£ relative luminance ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì:

```
Contrast Ratio = (L1 + 0.05) / (L2 + 0.05)
‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢ L1 = luminance ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤, L2 = luminance ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤

Relative Luminance = 0.2126 * R + 0.7152 * G + 0.0722 * B
‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢ R, G, B ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô linearization:
  - ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤ sRGB <= 0.03928 ‚Üí linear = sRGB / 12.92
  - ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤ sRGB > 0.03928 ‚Üí linear = ((sRGB + 0.055) / 1.055) ^ 2.4
```

### ‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö (‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á)

1. **‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏µ**: ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì contrast ratio ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á text color ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö background color
2. **‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ contrast ratio** ‡πÉ‡∏ô spec ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠ ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô: `#F0E8FF on #0D0A14 ‚Üí 15.2:1 ‚úÖ AAA`
3. **‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô AA**: ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏µ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ ‚Äî ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏ì‡∏ë‡πå
4. **‡∏™‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á contrast** ‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô preview spec info panel

### ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö

```
‚úÖ ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô:
  #F0E8FF on #0D0A14 ‚Üí 15.2:1 (AAA) ‚Äî primary text on dark bg
  #4ADE80 on #0D2818 ‚Üí 6.8:1 (AA)  ‚Äî positive text on green bg

‚ùå ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô:
  #7E6E98 on #1E1830 ‚Üí 2.8:1 (FAIL) ‚Äî ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏™‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô
```

### ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å color pair ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç:

- Text on background (‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å text level: primary, secondary, tertiary)
- Text on card surfaces
- Text on colored sections (DO/DON'T cards, alerts)
- Icon on background
- Button text on button background
- Placeholder text on input background

---

## ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç

1. **‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏à‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏î‡∏ú‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ**: ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏Ç‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠ (px, dp, pt, hex color)

### Flow ‡∏™‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏™‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô


‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ (‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏):

- **Focus Area**: ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏á‡∏ß‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏û‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏®‡∏©‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?

## Step 3: ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå 8 ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏¥

### 3.1 Visual Hierarchy & Layout (15%)
- ‡∏°‡∏µ clear hierarchy ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°? (primary ‚Üí secondary ‚Üí tertiary)
- Information architecture ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏°‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- Alignment ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ grid consistency
- White space usage ‚Äî ‡πÅ‡∏ô‡πà‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÇ‡∏•‡πà‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏õ?
- Gestalt principles: Proximity, Similarity, Continuity

### 3.2 Typography (10%)
- Type scale ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏°‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°? (‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î, ‡∏°‡∏µ hierarchy ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°)
- Font weight contrast ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏û‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- Line height / letter spacing ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô font families (‡∏¢‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏¢‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏î‡∏µ, ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô 2)

### 3.3 Color & Contrast (15%)
- **WCAG Contrast Check** (‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö):
  - Normal text: ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á >= 4.5:1 (AA)
  - Large text (>= 18pt bold / >= 24pt regular): ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á >= 3:1
  - UI components: ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á >= 3:1
- Color palette consistency ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏µ, ‡∏°‡∏µ system ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- Semantic color usage ‚Äî error=red, success=green ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- Dark mode compatibility (‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏µ)

### 3.4 Component Design (15%)
- ‡∏õ‡∏è‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° platform conventions ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°? (Jakob's Law)
- Button hierarchy ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°? (primary, secondary, tertiary)
- Input fields ‡∏°‡∏µ label, placeholder, helper text, error state ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- Card/container design consistent ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- Interactive elements ‡∏°‡∏µ visual affordance ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?

### 3.5 Spacing & Consistency (10%)
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ spacing system (4px/8px grid) ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- Padding/margin consistent ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- Component spacing ‡∏°‡∏µ pattern ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?

### 3.6 UX Heuristics ‚Äî Nielsen's 10 (20%)
- H1: Visibility of System Status ‚Äî ‡∏°‡∏µ feedback ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- H2: Match Real World ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏©‡∏≤‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- H3: User Control ‚Äî ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö/undo ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- H4: Consistency ‚Äî follow platform standards ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- H5: Error Prevention ‚Äî ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô error ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- H6: Recognition > Recall ‚Äî ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- H7: Flexibility ‚Äî ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö novice & expert ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- H8: Aesthetic & Minimalist ‚Äî ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- H9: Error Recovery ‚Äî error message ‡∏î‡∏µ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- H10: Help & Documentation ‚Äî ‡∏°‡∏µ guidance ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?

### 3.7 Accessibility (10%)
- Touch targets >= 44pt (iOS) / 48dp (Android)?
- Color not the only indicator?
- Screen reader friendly? (labels, roles)
- Sufficient contrast? (checked in 3.3)

### 3.8 Edge Cases (5%)
- Empty state ‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- Loading state ‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- Error state ‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- Long text / overflow handling?
- No data / no results state?

## Step 5: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Review Notes

### Output Format: HTML Review Notes (Preferred)

‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå `review-notes.html` ‡πÉ‡∏ô folder ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà review

**‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç: ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠ Designer ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¢ ‚Äî ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏î‡∏π‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î**

```
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ TABLE OF CONTENTS ‚Äî ‡∏Å‡∏î link ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ issue ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ

‚îÇ       ‚îÇ          + swatch ‡∏™‡∏µ + hex code + FAIL/PASS tag
‚îÇ       ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ FIX GUIDE ‚Äî ‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma / Design Tool
```

### Issue Card ‚Äî ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ö 3 ‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô:

1. **WHERE** (‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô?) ‚Äî **‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á (screenshot) ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß mark ‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á**:
   - ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ screenshot ‡∏°‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ folder ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö HTML ‚Üí `<img src="‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå.png">`
   - ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `sips -g pixelWidth -g pixelHeight` ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì % ‡∏ï‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏á
   - ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ CSS `position:relative` ‡∏ö‡∏ô container + `position:absolute` + `%` ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏á marker ‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ
   - Marker = div border ‡∏™‡∏µ + border-radius + label ID (C1, M1, m1) + pulse animation
   - ‡∏™‡∏µ marker: ‡πÅ‡∏î‡∏á (#EA244F) = Critical, ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏á (#D4920A) = Major, ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ß‡∏á (#7279FB) = Minor
   - **‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏î CSS mockup ‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà** ‚Äî ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô
   - ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ element ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á UI
   - ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏ section / component ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á

2. **VISUAL ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô/‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á** ‚Äî ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ:
   - Preview ‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á / ‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á ‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô-‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ
   - Contrast ratio tags (FAIL/PASS)
   - Swatch ‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° hex code + ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ token

3. **FIX GUIDE** (‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Designer) ‚Äî ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ:
   - ‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà Designer ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ
   - ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏©‡∏≤ design ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô "‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏µ fill ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô #D14A8A" ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏©‡∏≤‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î
   - ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≤ ‚Üí ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô (hex, px, token name)
   - ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏ token ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° Design System

### Annotated Overview (‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á report):
- ‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î ~320px width ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° marker ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î (‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å issue) ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß
- Legend ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ: ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å issue + ‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ

### ‡πÇ‡∏ó‡∏ô Designer-Friendly:
- **‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÇ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô/audit** ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÇ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏£‡πà‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥
- Section headers: "‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏î‡∏π‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô" / "‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î" / "‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏î‡∏π"
- ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å issue ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö "‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤..." + ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏‡∏ú‡∏• WHY ‡πÉ‡∏ô blockquote
- ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà "‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ" ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô "‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏î‡∏π‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¢ ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞..."

### Styling Guidelines:
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Design Tokens ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô CSS variables

## ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç

# User Flow / Information Architecture Skill

‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö User Flow ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Information Architecture ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö app/web ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö ‚Äî ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á journey

## Pipeline Position

```
Jira BA ‚Üí [IA + User Flow] ‚Üí UI Design ‚Üí QA Gate ‚Üí ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏ö
                ‚ñ≤ ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ
```

## Overall Flow

```
1. Requirements ‚Üí 2. Read Principles ‚Üí 3. Map IA ‚Üí 4. Design Flows ‚Üí 5. Generate Diagrams ‚Üí 6. Build in Figma (Optional) ‚Üí 7. ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏õ UI Design
```

1. **Requirements**: ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏à product, users, features (‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å **jira-req-analysis** skill)
2. **Read Principles**: ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô UX + navigation patterns
3. **Map IA**: ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏á Information Architecture
4. **Design Flows**: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á user flows ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö key tasks
5. **Generate Diagrams**: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á diagram ‡πÉ‡∏ô FigJam/Figma
6. **Build in Figma**: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á screen map ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma (optional)
7. **‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠**: ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á IA + Flows ‡πÑ‡∏õ **figma-ui-design-spec** skill ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á HTML preview

## Step 1: ‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏° Requirements

Requirements ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å:
- **Jira BA analysis** ‚Üí ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤ user ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô `jira-req-analysis` skill ‡∏°‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏µ structured data (User Stories, Screen List, State Matrix, Components, User Flow Summary, Edge Cases) ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ ‚Äî ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß ‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ç‡∏≤‡∏î
- **User ‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á** ‚Üí ‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á

‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ (‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏):

- **Product**: ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏õ/‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πá‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£? ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£?
- **Target Users**: ‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å (1-3 personas)
- **Platform**: Mobile (iOS/Android), Web, Desktop, Cross-platform?
- **Key Features**: features ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ (list ‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏°‡∏≤)
- **User Goals**: ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à? (top 3-5 goals)
- **Scope**: ‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á app ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏á module?
- **Reference**: ‡∏°‡∏µ app ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏î‡∏π‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô reference ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- **Existing Design**: ‡∏°‡∏µ Figma URL ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á design ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?

## Step 2: ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô Design Principles

‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô reference files:

```
references/ux-principles.md        ‚Üí ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠ (‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞ Hick's Law, Miller's Law, Jakob's Law)
references/material-design.md      ‚Üí Navigation patterns ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Android/Web
references/hig.md                  ‚Üí Navigation patterns ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö iOS
```

### Navigation Patterns ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ:

**iOS (HIG):**
- Tab Bar (3-5 items) + Navigation Stack ‚Äî most common
- Sidebar (iPad) ‚Üí Tab Bar (iPhone)
- Modal Sheets ‚Äî focused tasks

**Android (Material):**
- Bottom Navigation (3-5 items) ‚Äî compact
- Navigation Rail ‚Äî medium screens
- Navigation Drawer ‚Äî expanded screens

**Web:**
- Top Navigation Bar + Side Navigation
- Breadcrumbs for deep hierarchy
- Tab-based navigation for related content

---

## Step 3: Map Information Architecture

### 3.1 Feature Inventory

‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° features ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô categories:

```markdown
## Feature Inventory

| Category | Features | Priority |
|----------|----------|----------|
| Authentication | Login, Register, Forgot Password, Social Login | Must Have |
| Profile | View Profile, Edit Profile, Settings | Must Have |
| [Core Feature] | [list features] | Must Have |
| [Secondary] | [list features] | Should Have |
| [Nice-to-have] | [list features] | Could Have |
```

### 3.2 Content Model

‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î entities ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ relationships:

```markdown
## Content Model

| Entity | Key Attributes | Relationships |
|--------|---------------|---------------|
| User | name, email, avatar, role | has many Posts, has many Orders |
| Product | title, price, image, category | belongs to Category, has many Reviews |
| Order | items, total, status, date | belongs to User, has many Products |
```

### 3.3 Site Map / Screen Map

‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î hierarchy ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á screens:

```markdown
## Screen Map

### Level 0: Entry
- Splash / Onboarding

### Level 1: Main Navigation (Tab Bar / Bottom Nav)
- Home (Tab 1)
- Search (Tab 2)
- [Core Feature] (Tab 3)
- Profile (Tab 4)

### Level 2: Sub-screens
- Home ‚Üí Product Detail
- Home ‚Üí Category List ‚Üí Product List
- Search ‚Üí Search Results ‚Üí Product Detail
- Profile ‚Üí Settings ‚Üí Edit Profile
- Profile ‚Üí Order History ‚Üí Order Detail

### Level 3: Modals / Overlays
- Cart Sheet
- Filter Sheet
- Login Modal
```

### 3.4 Navigation Matrix

```markdown
## Navigation Matrix

| From \ To | Home | Search | Detail | Cart | Profile |
|-----------|------|--------|--------|------|---------|
| Home | ‚Äî | Tab | Push | Sheet | Tab |
| Search | Tab | ‚Äî | Push | Sheet | Tab |
| Detail | Back | ‚Äî | ‚Äî | Sheet | ‚Äî |
| Cart | Dismiss | ‚Äî | Push | ‚Äî | ‚Äî |
| Profile | Tab | Tab | ‚Äî | ‚Äî | ‚Äî |

Transition types: Tab (tab switch), Push (nav push), Sheet (modal), Back (pop), Dismiss (close modal)
```

---

## Step 4: Design User Flows

### 4.1 Identify Key Flows

‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å top 3-5 flows ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î:

```markdown
## Key User Flows

| # | Flow Name | User Goal | Priority | Complexity |
|---|-----------|-----------|----------|------------|
| 1 | Onboarding | ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏±‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô | Critical | Medium |
| 2 | [Core Task] | [goal] | Critical | High |
| 3 | Purchase | ‡∏ã‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à | Critical | High |
| 4 | Search & Filter | ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ | High | Medium |
| 5 | Account Management | ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ | Medium | Low |
```

### 4.2 Flow Diagram Format

‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ flow ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ format ‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ:

```markdown
### Flow: [Flow Name]

**User Goal**: [‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£]
**Entry Point**: [‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô]
**Success State**: [‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£]
**Happy Path Steps**: [‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô steps]

#### Happy Path:
1. [Screen A] ‚Üí User action: [action] ‚Üí
2. [Screen B] ‚Üí User action: [action] ‚Üí
3. [Screen C] ‚Üí Success ‚úì

#### Error/Alternative Paths:
- Step 2 error: [validation fail] ‚Üí Show inline error ‚Üí Retry
- Step 2 alternative: [‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏î back] ‚Üí Return to Screen A
- Step 3 timeout: [network error] ‚Üí Error state ‚Üí Retry button

#### Decision Points:
- [Screen B]: if logged in ‚Üí skip to Step 3; if not ‚Üí show login modal
- [Screen C]: if first time ‚Üí show tutorial; if returning ‚Üí skip

#### Edge Cases:
- No network ‚Üí Offline state with cached data
- Session expired ‚Üí Re-auth modal
- Deep link entry ‚Üí Skip to Step 2 with prefilled data
```

### 4.3 Flow Principles

‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å flow ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£:

- **Hick's Law**: ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ step ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô 5-7
- **Miller's Law**: ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô 7¬±2 chunks
- **Doherty Threshold**: ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ transition ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á < 400ms (perceived)
- **H1 - Visibility**: ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà step ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á flow
- **H3 - User Control**: ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å step ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö/undo
- **H5 - Error Prevention**: ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô error ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô submit

---

## Step 5: Generate Diagrams

### 5.1 ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Flow Diagram (‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Figma Remote MCP)

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `generate_diagram` ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Mermaid.js diagram:

```
generate_diagram({
  name: "User Registration Flow",
  mermaidSyntax: 'flowchart LR\n  A["Splash Screen"] -->|"Tap Get Started"| B["Sign Up Form"]\n  B -->|"Fill & Submit"| C{"Valid?"}\n  C -->|"Yes"| D["Verify Email"]\n  C -->|"No"| B\n  D -->|"Code Entered"| E["Welcome Screen"]\n  E -->|"Continue"| F["Home"]',
  userIntent: "Registration user flow diagram"
})
```

### Diagram Types ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ:

| Type | Mermaid Syntax | Use Case |
|------|---------------|----------|
| Flowchart | `flowchart LR` | User flows, task flows |
| Sequence | `sequenceDiagram` | API interactions, system flows |
| State Diagram | `stateDiagram-v2` | Screen states, component states |
| Gantt | `gantt` | Project timeline, feature roadmap |

### 5.2 Flow Diagram Best Practices

- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `flowchart LR` (left-to-right) ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö user flows
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `flowchart TD` (top-down) ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö decision trees
- ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å node ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ label ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏û‡∏π‡∏î
- Decision points ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ rhombus `{"Decision?"}`
- Color coding: green=success, red=error, blue=action
- ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ emoji ‡πÉ‡∏ô Mermaid syntax

### 5.3 Screen Map ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma (Optional ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ TalkToFigma MCP)

‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á visual screen map ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma:

```
1. ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á frame ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ screen (create_frame with name)
2. ‡πÉ‡∏™‡πà‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ screen (create_text)
3. ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ create_connections ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏° screens
4. ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î layout ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° hierarchy
```

## Step 6: Build Screen Map in Figma (Optional)

‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ screen map ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma:

‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á card ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ screen:

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `create_connections` ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°:
```

    { startNodeId: "home-id", endNodeId: "detail-id", text: "Tap Product" },
```

‡πÉ‡∏™‡πà annotations ‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢ flow logic:

```
set_multiple_annotations({
```

## Step 7: ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏õ UI Design

> "IA ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ User Flow ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö UI ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°? ‡∏ú‡∏°‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á HTML preview ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏î‡∏π‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¢"

‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ user ‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°:
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Step 1-6 ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô input ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö **figma-ui-design-spec** skill
- ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á: Screen Map, Navigation Matrix, User Flows (happy + error paths), Feature Inventory ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô requirements
- **figma-ui-design-spec** ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á HTML preview ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ screen
- ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ HTML ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏£‡πá‡∏à ‚Üí **html-qa-gate** ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏ö

### Data Handoff:

| Data | ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Step | ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏õ UI Design |
|------|---------|-------------------|

| Navigation Matrix | Step 3.4 | ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î transitions ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤ |

| Flow Diagrams | Step 5 | Reference ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö design |

## ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç

1. **Goal-Oriented**: ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å user goal ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà feature list
2. **Happy Path First**: ‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö happy path ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏î edge cases
3. **Minimal Steps**: ‡∏•‡∏î steps ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î (3-click rule ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô guideline)
4. **Clear Wayfinding**: ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ
5. **Consistent Navigation**: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ pattern ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á app
6. **Error Recovery**: ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å flow ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ error handling
7. **Platform Conventions**: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ navigation patterns ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° platform

# Accessibility Audit Skill

‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö Accessibility ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° WCAG 2.1 AA/AAA ‚Äî ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏¥ ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏™‡∏µ

## Overall Flow

```
1. Capture ‚Üí 2. Read Guidelines ‚Üí 3. Audit (7 Categories) ‚Üí 4. Score ‚Üí 5. Report ‚Üí 6. Fix
```

---

## Step 1: Capture Design

‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô Design Critique skill:

- **Figma URL** ‚Üí `get_screenshot`, `get_design_context`, `get_metadata`
- **Figma Selection** ‚Üí `read_my_design`, `scan_text_nodes`, `scan_nodes_by_types`
- **HTML Preview File** ‚Üí ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå `.html` ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ Read tool ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à contrast, touch targets, semantic HTML, ARIA attributes ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å source code ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á (‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô import Figma)
- **Context**: ‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ target WCAG level ‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠ AA ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ AAA?

---

## Step 2: ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô Guidelines

```
references/ux-principles.md     ‚Üí Accessibility sections
references/hig.md               ‚Üí iOS Accessibility guidelines
references/material-design.md   ‚Üí Material Accessibility guidelines
```

---

## Step 3: Audit ‚Äî ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à 7 ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏ß‡∏î

### Category 1: Color Contrast (WCAG 1.4.3 / 1.4.6)

**‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì Contrast Ratio:**
```
Contrast Ratio = (L1 + 0.05) / (L2 + 0.05)

Relative Luminance = 0.2126*R + 0.7152*G + 0.0722*B
‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢ R, G, B linearized:
  sRGB <= 0.03928 ‚Üí linear = sRGB / 12.92
  sRGB > 0.03928  ‚Üí linear = ((sRGB + 0.055) / 1.055) ^ 2.4
```

**‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏ì‡∏ë‡πå:**

| Element | AA (‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≥) | AAA (‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥) |
|---------|-------------|-------------|
| Normal text (< 18pt / < 14pt bold) | 4.5:1 | 7:1 |
| Large text (>= 18pt / >= 14pt bold) | 3:1 | 4.5:1 |
| UI components & icons | 3:1 | ‚Äî |
| Non-text contrast (borders, inputs) | 3:1 | ‚Äî |

**‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏π‡πà‡∏™‡∏µ:**
- Text on background (primary, secondary, tertiary, disabled)
- Text on cards / colored surfaces
- Text on images (‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ overlay)
- Icon on background
- Button text on button fill
- Placeholder text on input background
- Link text vs surrounding text
- Focus indicator contrast
- Border / divider visibility

**Output Table:**
```markdown
| Element | Foreground | Background | Ratio | Size | AA | AAA |
|---------|-----------|------------|-------|------|----|-----|
| Body text | #1A1A1A | #FFFFFF | 16.6:1 | 14px | PASS | PASS |
| Secondary text | #666666 | #FFFFFF | 5.7:1 | 14px | PASS | FAIL |
| Button label | #FFFFFF | #007AFF | 4.6:1 | 14pt bold | PASS | PASS |
| Placeholder | #999999 | #F5F5F5 | 2.1:1 | 14px | FAIL | FAIL |
```

### Category 2: Touch Targets (WCAG 2.5.5 / 2.5.8)

**‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏ì‡∏ë‡πå:**

| Platform | Minimum Size | Recommended | Spacing |
|----------|-------------|-------------|---------|
| iOS | 44 x 44pt | 56 x 56pt (primary) | >= 8pt |
| Android | 48 x 48dp | 56 x 56dp (primary) | >= 8dp |
| Web | 44 x 44px (WCAG) | 48 x 48px | >= 8px |

**‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à:**
- ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å button, link, icon button, toggle, checkbox, radio
- ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å interactive element ‡πÉ‡∏ô list (row tap area)
- Close buttons, back buttons
- Form elements (input tap area, dropdown)
- Navigation items (tab bar, nav bar buttons)

**Output Table:**
```markdown
| Element | Actual Size | Min Required | Status | Note |
|---------|------------|--------------|--------|------|
| Back button | 44x44pt | 44x44pt | PASS | ‚Äî |
| Star rating icon | 24x24pt | 44x44pt | FAIL | Add padding to 44pt |
| List row | 44pt height | 44pt | PASS | Full-width tap area |
```

### Category 3: Screen Reader / Assistive Technology (WCAG 1.1.1 / 4.1.2)

**‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à:**

| Check | Description | How to verify |
|-------|-------------|---------------|
| Image alt text | ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å meaningful image ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ alt text | ‡∏î‡∏π image nodes |
| Decorative images | ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á hide ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å screen reader | ‡∏î‡∏π‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô decorative ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏° |
| Button labels | ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å button ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ accessible label | ‡∏î‡∏π text content |
| Icon-only buttons | ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ accessibilityLabel | ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πá‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏µ visible label ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ aria-label |
| Form labels | ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å input ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á associate ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö label | ‡∏î‡∏π label-input relationship |
| Heading structure | ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ proper heading hierarchy (h1‚Üíh2‚Üíh3) | ‡∏î‡∏π text hierarchy |
| Reading order | ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà make sense | ‡∏î‡∏π visual order vs DOM order |
| Focus order | tab order ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á logical | ‡∏î‡∏π interactive element order |
| Link purpose | link text ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏õ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà "click here") | ‡∏î‡∏π link text |
| Error announcements | error ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á announce ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ screen reader | ‡∏î‡∏π error handling |

**Output Table:**
```markdown
| Element | Check | Status | Issue | Fix |
|---------|-------|--------|-------|-----|
| Search icon | Label | FAIL | No accessible label | Add "Search" label |
| Hero image | Alt text | FAIL | Missing alt | Add descriptive alt |
| Email field | Form label | PASS | Has visible label | ‚Äî |
| "Click here" link | Link purpose | FAIL | Vague text | Change to "View pricing" |
```

### Category 4: Color Independence (WCAG 1.4.1)

‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ö‡πà‡∏á‡∏ä‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß:

**‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à:**
- Error states: ‡∏°‡∏µ icon ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ text ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏ö ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏™‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏î‡∏á?
- Success states: ‡∏°‡∏µ checkmark ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏™‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß?
- Required fields: ‡∏°‡∏µ * ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ text ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏™‡∏µ?
- Active/selected states: ‡∏°‡∏µ indicator ‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏µ?
- Charts/graphs: ‡∏°‡∏µ pattern/label ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏™‡∏µ?
- Links in text: ‡∏°‡∏µ underline ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏ü‡πâ‡∏≤?
- Status badges: ‡∏°‡∏µ icon + text ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏™‡∏µ?

**Color Blindness Simulation:**

‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ design ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö color vision deficiencies:
- Protanopia (red-blind, ~1% males)
- Deuteranopia (green-blind, ~1% males)
- Tritanopia (blue-blind, rare)
- Achromatopsia (total color blind, very rare)

‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏á:
- Red vs Green (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô error vs success) ‚Äî ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ shape/icon ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢
- Red vs Brown, Green vs Brown
- Blue vs Purple
- Light Green vs Light Yellow

### Category 5: Keyboard Navigation (WCAG 2.1.1 / 2.1.2 / 2.4.7)

‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Web / Desktop:

**‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à:**
| Check | Description |
|-------|-------------|
| All interactive reachable | ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å interactive element ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á tab ‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ |
| Focus visible | focus indicator ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î (contrast >= 3:1) |
| Focus order | tab order logical ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° visual layout |
| No keyboard trap | ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å element ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ (especially modals) |
| Skip links | ‡∏°‡∏µ "Skip to main content" link |
| Shortcuts | keyboard shortcuts ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà conflict ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö screen reader |
| Modal focus trap | focus ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á trap ‡πÉ‡∏ô modal ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î |

**Focus Indicator Style:**
```
Focus ring: 2px solid, contrast >= 3:1 vs background AND focused element
Recommended: #005FCC (blue) on light, #66B2FF on dark
Offset: 2px from element edge
```

### Category 6: Text & Readability (WCAG 1.4.4 / 1.4.8 / 1.4.12)

**‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à:**
| Check | Criteria |
|-------|----------|
| Text resize | ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö zoom 200% ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏¢ content |

| Letter spacing | ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á adjust ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà lock ‡πÉ‡∏ô image) |
| Text alignment | ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà justify (justified text ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å) |
| Line length | 45-75 characters per line (optimal: 66) |
| Font size minimum | >= 16px/16sp/16pt ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö body text |
| Dynamic Type (iOS) | ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Dynamic Type scaling |
| Text in images | ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏µ‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ real text ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô |

‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç:

- `set_padding(nodeId, ...)` ‚Äî ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° padding ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ tap area ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô

- `set_text_content(nodeId, text)` ‚Äî ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ link text ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ descriptive

**Visual indicator fixes:**

- `create_rectangle(...)` ‚Äî ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° icons/shapes ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏µ

# Design System Creation Skill

‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Design System ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö ‚Äî ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà tokens, typography scale, color system, components ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á documentation ‚Äî ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma

## Overall Flow

```
1. Requirements ‚Üí 2. Read References ‚Üí 3. Define Foundations ‚Üí 4. Design Components ‚Üí 5. Preview (HTML) ‚Üí 6. Import to Figma (HTML to Figma MCP) ‚Üí 7. Document
```

---

## Step 1: ‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏° Requirements

‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ:

- **Brand**: ‡∏°‡∏µ brand guidelines ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°? (‡∏™‡∏µ, font, logo)
- **Platform**: Mobile, Web, Cross-platform?
- **Base System**: ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Material Design / HIG / ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏®‡∏π‡∏ô‡∏¢‡πå?
- **Scale**: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏ô? ‡∏Å‡∏µ‡πà product? (‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ã‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô)
- **Components Needed**: ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ components ‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£‡∏ö‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á? (‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥?)
- **Theme**: ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Light/Dark mode ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- **Existing Design**: ‡∏°‡∏µ Figma URL ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á design ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?

---

## Step 2: ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô References

```

```

## Step 3: Define Foundations (Design Tokens)

### 3.1 Color System

**Step-by-step:**

1. **‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å Primary Color** ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å brand (‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà)
2. **Generate Color Scale** ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ hue:
   ```
   [color]-50:  lightest (background tint)
   [color]-100: very light
   [color]-200: light
   [color]-300: medium light
   [color]-400: medium
   [color]-500: base (primary)
   [color]-600: medium dark
   [color]-700: dark
   [color]-800: very dark
   [color]-900: darkest
   [color]-950: near black
   ```

3. **‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î Semantic Colors**:
   ```markdown
   | Token | Light Mode | Dark Mode | Usage |
   |-------|-----------|-----------|-------|
   | color-primary | blue-600 | blue-400 | Primary actions, links |
   | color-on-primary | white | blue-950 | Text on primary |
   | color-secondary | gray-600 | gray-400 | Secondary actions |
   | color-error | red-600 | red-400 | Error states |
   | color-warning | amber-600 | amber-400 | Warning states |
   | color-success | green-600 | green-400 | Success states |
   | color-info | blue-500 | blue-300 | Informational |
   | color-surface | white | gray-900 | Backgrounds |
   | color-on-surface | gray-900 | gray-50 | Primary text |
   | color-on-surface-variant | gray-600 | gray-400 | Secondary text |
   | color-outline | gray-300 | gray-700 | Borders |
   | color-outline-variant | gray-200 | gray-800 | Subtle borders |
   ```

4. **WCAG Contrast Check** (‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö):
   ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏π‡πà semantic color:
   ```
   color-on-surface on color-surface ‚Üí ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á >= 4.5:1 (AA)
   color-on-primary on color-primary ‚Üí ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á >= 4.5:1 (AA)
   color-on-surface-variant on color-surface ‚Üí ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á >= 4.5:1 (AA)
   ```

### 3.2 Typography Scale

**‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î Type Scale (‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö Figma Text Styles):**

```markdown
| Token | Size | Weight | Line Height | Usage |
|-------|------|--------|-------------|-------|
| Heading.1 | 48px | Bold (700) | 58px | Page titles, hero text |
| Heading.2 | 40px | Bold (700) | 52px | Section headers |
| Heading.3 | 32px | Bold (700) | 40px | Sub-section headers |
| Heading.4 | 28px | Bold (700) | 36px | Card titles, dialog headers |
| Heading.5 | 24px | Bold (700) | 32px | Small headings, list titles |
| Label.1 | 20px | Bold (700) | 28px | Large labels |
| Label.2 | 18px | Bold (700) | 26px | Medium labels |
| Label.3 | 16px | Bold (700) | 24px | Buttons, standard labels |
| Label.4 | 14px | Bold (700) | 22px | Small labels, tags |
| Label.5 | 12px | Bold (700) | 20px | Micro labels, badges |
| Caption.1 | 20px | Regular (400) | 36px | Large body text |
| Caption.2 | 18px | Regular (400) | 26px | Medium body text |
| Caption.3 | 16px | Regular (400) | 24px | Standard body text |
| Caption.4 | 14px | Regular (400) | 22px | Small text, captions |
| Caption.5 | 12px | Regular (400) | 20px | Micro text, footnotes |
```

**Font Family:**
- Primary: LINE Seed Sans TH
- Weights: Regular (400), Bold (700), ExtraBold (800)
- Fallback: sans-serif

### 3.3 Spacing System

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ 4px base unit:

```markdown
| Token | Value | Usage |
|-------|-------|-------|
| space-0 | 0px | ‚Äî |
| space-1 | 4px | Icon padding, micro gaps |
| space-2 | 8px | Inline elements, tight |
| space-3 | 12px | List item internal |
| space-4 | 16px | Content padding (default) |
| space-5 | 20px | Card padding |
| space-6 | 24px | Section gaps |
| space-8 | 32px | Large gaps |
| space-10 | 40px | Section breaks |
| space-12 | 48px | Page sections |
| space-16 | 64px | Hero spacing |
| space-20 | 80px | Page top/bottom |
```

### 3.4 Shape (Corner Radius)

```markdown
| Token | Value | Usage |
|-------|-------|-------|
| radius-none | 0px | Sharp corners |
| radius-xs | 4px | Tags, badges, chips |
| radius-sm | 8px | Buttons, inputs, small cards |
| radius-md | 12px | Cards, dialogs |
| radius-lg | 16px | Large cards, FABs |
| radius-xl | 24px | Bottom sheets |
| radius-full | 9999px | Pills, avatars, circles |
```

### 3.5 Elevation

```markdown
| Token | Shadow | Usage |
|-------|--------|-------|
| elevation-0 | none | Flat surfaces |
| elevation-1 | 0 1px 3px rgba(0,0,0,0.12) | Cards (rest) |
| elevation-2 | 0 4px 6px rgba(0,0,0,0.1) | Dropdowns, popovers |
| elevation-3 | 0 8px 16px rgba(0,0,0,0.1) | FAB, bottom sheets |
| elevation-4 | 0 12px 24px rgba(0,0,0,0.12) | Dialogs, modals |
```

## Step 4: Design Components

### Atomic Design Hierarchy

```
Atoms ‚Üí Molecules ‚Üí Organisms ‚Üí Templates ‚Üí Pages
```

### 4.1 Atoms (‡∏û‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô)

| Component | Variants | States |
|-----------|----------|--------|
| Button | filled, outlined, text, tonal, icon | default, hover, pressed, focused, disabled, loading |
| Icon Button | filled, outlined, standard | default, hover, pressed, focused, disabled |
| Text Field | filled, outlined | default, focused, filled, error, disabled |
| Checkbox | ‚Äî | unchecked, checked, indeterminate, disabled |
| Radio Button | ‚Äî | unselected, selected, disabled |
| Toggle/Switch | ‚Äî | off, on, disabled |
| Badge | number, dot | ‚Äî |
| Chip | assist, filter, input, suggestion | default, selected, disabled |
| Divider | full-width, inset | ‚Äî |
| Avatar | image, initials, icon | sizes: sm, md, lg |

### 4.2 Molecules (‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å atoms)

| Component | Description |
|-----------|-------------|
| Search Bar | input + icon + clear button |
| List Item | avatar + text + trailing action |
| Form Field | label + input + helper text + error text |
| Menu Item | icon + label + shortcut |
| Snackbar / Toast | text + optional action button |
| Tab | icon + label + indicator |

### 4.3 Organisms (complex components)

| Component | Description |
|-----------|-------------|
| Top App Bar | nav icon + title + action icons |
| Bottom Navigation | 3-5 tab items |
| Navigation Rail | icon + label items |
| Navigation Drawer | header + menu items |
| Card | header + content + actions |
| Dialog / Modal | title + body + action buttons |
| Bottom Sheet | handle + content |
| Data Table | header + rows + pagination |
| Form | grouped form fields + submit |

### Component Spec Template

‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ component ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î:

```markdown
## Component: [Name]

### Anatomy
[‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ sub-elements]

### Variants
| Variant | Visual Difference | When to Use |
|---------|------------------|-------------|
| Filled | Solid background | Primary actions |
| Outlined | Border only | Secondary actions |

### Sizes
| Size | Height | Padding | Font | Icon |
|------|--------|---------|------|------|
| Small | 32px | 12px H | label-md | 16px |
| Medium | 40px | 16px H | label-lg | 20px |
| Large | 48px | 20px H | body-lg | 24px |

### States
| State | Background | Text | Border | Opacity |
|-------|-----------|------|--------|---------|
| Default | primary | on-primary | ‚Äî | 100% |
| Hover | primary-dark | on-primary | ‚Äî | 100% |
| Pressed | primary-darker | on-primary | ‚Äî | 100% |
| Focused | primary | on-primary | focus-ring | 100% |
| Disabled | on-surface | on-surface | ‚Äî | 38% |
| Loading | primary | ‚Äî | ‚Äî | 70% + spinner |

### Accessibility
- Min touch target: 48x48dp / 44x44pt
- Focus indicator: 2px ring
- Disabled: opacity 38%, not focusable
- Screen reader: role="button", aria-label if icon-only

### Spacing Rules
- Internal padding: [values]
- Min gap between buttons: space-2 (8px)
- Margin from screen edge: space-4 (16px)
```

## Step 5: Preview (Static HTML)

‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á HTML preview ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á Design System Overview ‚Äî ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ô browser ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ:

### Preview ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ:

1. **Color Palette** ‚Äî ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å color token ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° hex (CSS Variables)
2. **Typography Scale** ‚Äî ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å type style (Google Fonts: LINE Seed Sans TH)
3. **Spacing Scale** ‚Äî visual representation
4. **Component Gallery** ‚Äî ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å component, ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å variant, ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å state
5. **Light/Dark Toggle** ‚Äî ‡∏™‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö theme ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ (vanilla JS)
6. **Component State Switcher** ‚Äî ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô state ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ (vanilla JS)

### Guidelines:

- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ **CSS Variables** ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° Design Tokens (`references/design-tokens.md`)
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ **flexbox/grid** layout ‚Üí ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Auto Layout ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma
- ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á **class names** ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢ ‚Üí ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Figma layer names
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ **semantic HTML** (`<header>`, `<section>`, `<main>`)
- **‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ** React, Vue, ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ JS framework ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ vanilla JS ‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ **inline SVG** ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ placeholder ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö icons

‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠: `[system-name]-design-system-preview.html`

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ **html-to-design MCP** ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á HTML ‡πÑ‡∏õ Figma ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á:


   ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ serve file ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `import_url`:
   ```
   import_url({ url: "http://localhost:3000/design-system-preview.html", name: "Design System" })
   ```
3. Plugin ‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á HTML ‚Üí Figma layers ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥
4. ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö fine-tune ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma:
   - ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à font ‚Äî ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô LINE Seed Sans TH ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£
   - ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à sizing mode (FILL/HUG/FIXED)
   - ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö layer names ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£
   - ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á components, variants, styles ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° design system

## ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç

1. **Token-First**: ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î tokens ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö component
2. **Consistent Naming**: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `{category}-{property}-{variant}` ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠
3. **Scalable**: ‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° variant/component ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢
4. **Accessible by Default**: ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å component ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô WCAG AA
5. **Theme-Ready**: ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å color token ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ Light + Dark mode
6. **Platform-Aware**: ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö sizing/spacing ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° platform (pt vs dp vs px)
7. **Document Everything**: ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å component ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ usage guideline
8. **Less is More**: ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å minimal set ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°

# Responsive / Adaptive Design Skill

‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö UI ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏ö‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠ ‚Äî ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Mobile ‡πÄ‡∏•‡πá‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏à‡∏ô Desktop ‡∏à‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢ frames ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma

## Overall Flow

```
1. Requirements ‚Üí 2. Read References ‚Üí 3. Define Breakpoints ‚Üí 4. Design Adaptation Rules ‚Üí 5. Preview (HTML) ‚Üí 6. Import to Figma (HTML to Figma MCP)
```

## Step 1: ‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏° Requirements

‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ:

- **Primary Platform**: Mobile-first ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Desktop-first?
- **Target Breakpoints**: ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î? (Mobile / Tablet / Desktop / Large Desktop)
- **Screen/Feature**: ‡∏à‡∏∞ responsive ‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£? (‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß / ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á app)
- **Content Priority**: content ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏ö‡∏ô mobile?
- **Navigation**: ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô navigation pattern ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° size ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- **Existing Design**: ‡∏°‡∏µ Figma URL ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á design ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà (size ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß) ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- **Framework**: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ CSS framework ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô? (Tailwind, Bootstrap, custom)
