## Step 6: Output

### Output Format: HTML Usability Test Plan

‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå `usability-test-plan.html` ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á:

1. **Test Overview** ‚Äî goals, method, timeline, participants
2. **Participant Profile** ‚Äî demographics + screener questions
3. **Task Scenarios** ‚Äî ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å task ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° scenario + success criteria
4. **Moderator Script** ‚Äî script ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏û‡πå‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ
5. **Data Collection Sheet** ‚Äî ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á record data per participant
6. **Analysis Framework** ‚Äî severity scale + finding template
7. **Timeline** ‚Äî recruitment ‚Üí testing ‚Üí analysis ‚Üí report
8. **Printable Consent Form** ‚Äî form ‡∏Ç‡∏≠ consent ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å

### Alternative Output: Markdown
‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô markdown ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Notion/Confluence

---

## ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç

1. **5 Users Enough**: 5 ‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ 85% (Nielsen)
2. **Test Early, Test Often**: ‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö lo-fi ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¢
3. **Observe, Don't Lead**: ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏ö‡πâ ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢ (‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡πÜ)
4. **Think Aloud**: ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ user ‡∏û‡∏π‡∏î‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏î ‚Äî data ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î
5. **Behavior > Opinion**: ‡∏™‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà user ‡∏ó‡∏≥ ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà user ‡∏û‡∏π‡∏î
6. **No Bias**: ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏° leading questions ("‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏ä‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?")
7. **Iterate Fast**: test ‚Üí find ‚Üí fix ‚Üí test again ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô launch

## Step 1: ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Design

**‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Figma:**

## Step 2: ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå Design

### 2.1 Screen Inventory

‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å screen + states:

| # | Screen | States | Components | Notes |
|---|--------|--------|------------|-------|
| 1 | Login | default, filled, error, loading | Input√ó2, Button, Link | Social login options |
| 2 | Home | default, loading, empty, error | Header, Card√óN, TabBar | Infinite scroll |

### 2.2 Component Inventory

‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å component ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ:

| Component | Variants | States | Props |
|-----------|----------|--------|-------|
| Button | Primary, Secondary, Tertiary | Default, Pressed, Disabled, Loading | label, icon?, size, isLoading |
| Input | Text, Password, Email, Search | Default, Focused, Filled, Error, Disabled | label, placeholder, helper, error, type |
| Card | Default, Compact, Featured | Default, Pressed | title, subtitle, image?, badge? |

### 2.3 Token Mapping

‡∏à‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏π‡πà design values ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö tokens:

| Property | Design Value | Token Name | CSS Variable |
|----------|-------------|------------|-------------|
| Primary color | #EC599D | primary/bg/mid | --color-primary |
| Body text | #1B1D22 | gray-neutral/fg/high | --color-text-primary |
| Card padding | 16px | spacing-4 | --spacing-4 |
| Card radius | 12px | radius-lg | --radius-lg |
| Body font | 16px/24px Regular | caption-3 | --font-body |

### 3.3 Interaction Spec (Per Component)

| Element | Trigger | Action | Animation | Duration |
|---------|---------|--------|-----------|----------|
| Login Button | Tap | Validate ‚Üí API call ‚Üí Navigate | Press scale ‚Üí Loading ‚Üí Success | 100ms ‚Üí ‚àû ‚Üí 300ms |
| Email Input | Focus | Show keyboard, scroll into view | Border color change | 200ms |
| Password Eye | Tap | Toggle visibility | Icon swap | instant |
| Forgot PW | Tap | Navigate to reset flow | Push right | 300ms |
| Social Login | Tap | Open OAuth webview | Scale press ‚Üí slide up | 100ms ‚Üí 300ms |

### 3.4 Responsive Behavior

| Breakpoint | Layout Change | Notes |
|------------|--------------|-------|
| Mobile (< 640px) | Single column, full-width buttons | Default design |
| Tablet (768px) | Center content, max-width 400px | Card-like container |
| Desktop (1024px+) | Split layout: illustration left, form right | 50/50 split |

### 3.5 Edge Cases & Error States

| Case | UI Behavior | Copy | Design |
|------|------------|------|--------|
| Empty email | Inline error below input | "‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•" | Red border + error text |
| Invalid email format | Inline error | "‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á" | Red border |
| Wrong password | Inline error + shake | "‡∏£‡∏´‡∏±‡∏™‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á" | Shake animation 300ms |
| Network error | Toast notification | "‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ ‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á" | Error toast bottom |
| Server 500 | Full-screen error | "‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î" + retry button | Error illustration |
| Account locked | Alert dialog | "‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏•‡πá‡∏≠‡∏Ñ" + support link | Warning dialog |
| Long email (overflow) | Text ellipsis | ‚Äî | Truncate with ... |

## Step 4: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Handoff Document

### Handoff Document Structure

```
handoff-doc.html
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ OVERVIEW
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Feature summary (1-2 sentences)
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Screen list + state matrix
‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Tech requirements (platform, dependencies)
‚îÇ
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ DESIGN TOKENS
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Colors used (with CSS variables)
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Typography used (with token names)
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Spacing values (with token names)
‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Other tokens (radius, shadow, etc.)
‚îÇ
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ SCREEN SPECS (per screen)
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Full screenshot + annotated measurements
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Component breakdown (which components used)
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Spacing diagram (all margins, paddings, gaps)
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Responsive behavior table
‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Edge cases + error states
‚îÇ
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ COMPONENT SPECS (per component)
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Visual spec (size, colors, typography)
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ All states (default, hover, pressed, disabled, error, loading)
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Props / variants table
‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Interaction spec (triggers, animations, durations)
‚îÇ
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ INTERACTION SPEC
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Screen transition map
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Gesture spec (if mobile)
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Loading states spec
‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Animation timing table
‚îÇ
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ ASSET LIST
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Icons needed (with size + format)
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Images needed (with dimensions + format)
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Illustrations (with source)
‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Fonts (with weights + source)
‚îÇ
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ API MAPPING (if known)
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Screen ‚Üí API endpoint mapping
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Form field ‚Üí API field mapping
‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Error code ‚Üí UI state mapping
‚îÇ
‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ CHECKLIST
    ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Implementation checklist (per screen)
    ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Accessibility requirements
    ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Testing scenarios
```

### Asset Export Spec

| Asset | Format | Sizes | Naming |
|-------|--------|-------|--------|
| App icon | PNG | 1024√ó1024, @1x @2x @3x | app-icon |
| Tab icons | SVG or PNG | 24√ó24 @1x, @2x, @3x | icon-{name} |
| Illustrations | SVG or PNG | Original + @2x | illust-{name} |
| Photos | JPEG/WebP | Multiple sizes | photo-{name}-{size} |
| Logos | SVG | Original | logo-{variant} |

### Implementation Notes

‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà dev ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà design ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô:

```markdown
## Notes for Developers

### Behavior Notes
- [Form] Auto-save draft ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å 30 ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ
- [List] Infinite scroll ‚Äî load 20 items per page
- [Image] Lazy load images outside viewport
- [Input] Debounce search input 300ms
- [Button] Disable after tap until API responds (prevent double-submit)

### Accessibility Notes
- All interactive elements: min 44√ó44pt touch target
- All images: require alt text
- Form errors: announce via screen reader (aria-live="assertive")
- Color is not the only indicator: use icons + text alongside colors
- Support Dynamic Type / font scaling

### Performance Notes
- Use skeleton screens during API calls
- Cache API responses where appropriate
- Optimize images (WebP, lazy load, srcset)
- Preload critical fonts
```

---

## Step 5: Output

### Output Format: HTML Handoff Document

‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå `handoff-[feature-name].html` ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á:

1. **Overview** ‚Äî feature summary + screen list
2. **Token Table** ‚Äî ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å token ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° CSS variable + preview ‡∏™‡∏µ
3. **Screen Specs** ‚Äî annotated screenshots + spacing diagrams
4. **Component Specs** ‚Äî visual spec + states + props
5. **Interaction Specs** ‚Äî transitions + animations + gestures
6. **Asset List** ‚Äî ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å asset ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á export
7. **Edge Cases** ‚Äî ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å error/empty/loading state
8. **Implementation Checklist** ‚Äî dev ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ check ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ implement ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏£‡πá‡∏à

### Styling Guidelines
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Design Tokens ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö
- Component specs ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ real design values (px, hex, token names)
- ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å measurement ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô ‚Äî ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ "‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì"
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ visual diagrams ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà text descriptions

---

## ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç

1. **No Ambiguity**: ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å value ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏ exact (px, hex, token name) ‚Äî ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏° "‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì"
2. **All States Covered**: ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å component ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å state (default, hover, pressed, disabled, error, loading)
3. **Edge Cases First**: Edge cases ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ happy path ‚Äî dev ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ design ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ error/empty/offline
4. **Token-Based**: ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å value ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á map ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö design token ‚Äî ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà hardcode
5. **Visual > Text**: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ annotated screenshots + diagrams ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢
6. **Dev Language**: ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏©‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà dev ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏à (px, rem, CSS properties)
7. **Single Source of Truth**: Handoff doc ‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠ "‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á" ‚Äî ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤ Figma ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö doc ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏¢‡∏∂‡∏î doc
8. **Checklist-Driven**: dev ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á check ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å item ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏™‡πà‡∏á review

A ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏®‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ó‡πå‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç
